msg:The overall impression of Regent Hotel is quite good to me, worthy of five-star praise. There are two points of praise. The first is that the hotel waiter reminded me to bring an umbrella in a note; the second is that the Regent Club staff can remember what drinks we had the day before, and asked us if we need to try other drinks, which proves that The staff at the club are very caring. But there are two criticisms, and I hope it can be improved. First, when we just arrived at the entrance of the hotel, I don‚Äôt know whether it was because we didn‚Äôt pay attention or for other reasons. My child and I each dragged a suitcase and walked from the subway station, but no one came to help take it or even came to ask; the second Second, when taking a shower, I found that there was not enough shower gel at the end. It is reasonable that every guest should check whether there are enough cleaning supplies, paper towels, mini bar, etc. after checking out. But it doesn't affect my five-star praise for your hotel, I hope you can do better.
